< Text>
This is by far the worst Kaiser Pharmacy I have experienced. I was getting my sons medication here for his epholepsy for over a year. Then out of the blue the pharmacist, not the doctor or the pharmacy, but the lead pharmacist decided to change the manufacturer supplier for his Depakote. The one thing all 4 of my son's doctors have told me is to never change suppliers of a generic medication. The reason is the medication makeup is by law, allowed to change by 10% from generic to name brand. So from generic to generic you could possibly see a 20% difference in dosage. With seizure medications this big of a change could actually bring on a seizure. I don't take chances with my son's health. I did everything the head pharmacist asked including having his Dr. spacificaly wright the script for the brand name medication.  He was prescribed this brand and it has been working flowlessley sense his second seizure.  I made no less than 8 visits to this pharmacy and had my son's Dr make 4 attempts to satisfy the lead Pharmacist demands. No luck. All my fears of THIS lancaster pharmacy and the lead pharmacist were verified. Both the Panorama City and Palmdale Kaiser pharmacies said the same. They have both correctly filled his scripts with zero trouble and both have confirmed the notes that show that the Lancaster pharmacy has taken it upon them selves to change his supplier. With no regard for the patient and the patients health. The big difference is cost. To save a buck he would put my son at risk. These are the BEST donuts I've ever tasted!!! They are fresh, soft and they are smooth while eating. They also give you a couple of donut holes with your order and OMG!!!! THE BEST! Honestly, they taste like Fruit Loops and it just melts in your mouth! I normally get regular chocolate, chocolate bar with Bulgarian creme, and glaze. I've tried Red's Donuts and they are alright. They have a harder dough texture and just doesn't taste fresh to me.<//review>

< text>
A friend recommended CJ Deli the last time I was in town. I've been running around all day- and was starving today, thankfully I remembered the tip of CJ Deli.
I did a quick yelp search to make sure they were open and to check the menu. Yes- they are open, and the food sounded great.
My friend and I picked up 2 sandwiches for lunch for takeaway. She had the Natural sandwich and I had the vegetarian.
The natural comes with 2 kinds of cheese- American and Swiss. My friend said she didn't want the Swiss, they offered her an extra slice of American cheese. We got the small sandwiches- still plenty big. We each still have 1/2 to enjoy later.
The vegetarian is really good- I loved the flavors. The bread was so yummy. It's nice and soft- tasted homemade. The sandwich has sprouts, egg, cucumber, and avocado. They also have free add ons  onions, pickles, and jalape√±os
The restaurant was very clean, staff was very friendly and efficient.
Plenty of parking available as well.
They are now open for dine in as well as offer takeout< /text>

< Review>
There are a lot of things to say about this furniture store.....

If you look at a lot of the reviews that are 5 stars a lot of the profiles have ONLY reviewed for this store. Pretty sure they buy reviews considering that they go after those who do write bad reviews and ask them to take it down.

If you look them up on the Better Business Bureau you can see
"Complaints we have received for Mattress & Furniture Express
contain similar allegations. Complainants have alleged the company
delays delivery of orders by weeks or months and refuses to cancel
their orders or provide refunds. They also allege receiving orders with
parts missing or broken"

The company has not responded back to the Better Business Bureau.

This is a a family business that have several different locations. This particular location is managed by Amrit and is the owner. If you are trying to get direct help don't go in when it is packed. There is not enough staff to manage the amount of people who go in. More than half the staff DOES NOT WEAR MASKS even though they have signs on the door before you enter that you need one. As you can imagine they do not enforce this policy on their customers either.

A guy who does not wear a mask who I believe is named Elliot (who also does not wear a mask) pressures you to buy, tries to get you to sign up for their "loan program", and is constantly distracted with other customers and gives inaccurate prices which later have to be corrected by Amrit in which he gives it for a higher price.

These people are so desperate to make a sale and do not prioritize customer service, when I arrived they were so busy, two people were walking out. They young lady who works there literally ran out to them and tried to get them to apply to their credit financing option and they look disgusted and just left.

The only positive I have is that the people that delivered our furniture were nice but, they were not wearing masks which is very alarming as they were entering our home.

Save yourself the hassle and go to a different furniture store.</Review>
